### 4.5.5.3 CSI-RS Multiplexing

#### 4.5.5.3.1 General

**4.5.5.3.1.0-3**  (ID: `12563356`)

General
5G-L1-DL(BB) shall support the following multiplexing between channels and CSI-RS signals:

* For all slot types except ssBurst slot:

o TDM shall be supported between Cx and other UL or DL channels.

o FDM shall be supported between Ct and PDSCH.

* For ssBurst slot in case of FR1 TDD and FDD:

o TDM shall be supported between CSI-RS signal, PDCCH, PDSCH, SSB and PUCCH.

o FDM shall be supported between Ct and PDSCH.

o FDM shall be supported between Cb and SSB in FR1 TDD (See [11444506](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e_rjXPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

* For ssBurst slot in case of FR2 TDD:

o TDM shall be supported between Ct and SSB of case E with eCPRI fronthaul.

Note:

* TDM: Time division multiplexing
* FDM: Frequency Division Multiplexing
* Ca: CSI-RS for measurement
* Ct: CSI-RS for tracking
* Cb: CSI-RS for beam management
* Cx: CSI-RS for either measurement or tracking is transmitted.

Note: CSI-RS for beam management is not supported in TDD FR1 eCPRI-7-2e.

The supported L1 HW(s) are shown in the following table:

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Technology | Loner | Loki | Thor BB | Odin BB |
| FR1-FDD-CPRI | Supported | Supported | Supported | **[CB012115-SR-JA, CB012115-SR-JB] Supported** [End CB012115-SR-JA, CB012115-SR-JB]\*\*\*\* |
| FR1-FDD-OBSAI | - | Supported | Supported | - |
| FR1-FDD-7-2a-eCPRI | - | Supported | Supported | **[CB012115-SR-LA] Supported** [End CB012115-SR-LA]\*\*\*\* |
| FR1-TDD-CPRI | Supported | Supported | Supported | - |
| FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI | Supported | Supported | Supported | **[CB012115-SR-IA] Supported** [End CB012115-SR-IA]\*\*\*\* |
| FR2-TDD-CPRI | Supported | - | - | - |
| FR2-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI | Supported | Supported | Supported | - |

---

#### 4.5.5.3.2 Frequency multiplexing within PRB(s) between CSI-RS for measurement(s)

**4.5.5.3.2.0-5**  (ID: `13424256`)

Frequency multiplexing within PRB(s) between CSI-RS for measurement(s)
13424256:
Frequency multiplexing within PRB(s) between CSI-RS for measurement(s)
13424256:
Frequency multiplexing within PRB(s) between CSI-RS for measurement(s)
13424256:
Frequency multiplexing within PRB(s) between CSI-RS for measurement(s)
13424256:
Frequency multiplexing within PRB(s) between CSI-RS for measurement(s)
13424256:
Frequency multiplexing within PRB(s) between CSI-RS for measurement(s)
13424256:
Frequency multiplexing within PRB(s) between CSI-RS for measurement(s)
13424256:
Frequency multiplexing within PRB(s) between CSI-RS for measurement(s)
13424256:
Frequency multiplexing within PRB(s) between CSI-RS for measurement(s)
13424256:
Frequency multiplexing within PRB(s) between CSI-RS for measurement(s)
13424256:
Frequency multiplexing within PRB(s) between CSI-RS for measurement(s)
5G-L1-DL shall support multiplexing between two CSI-RS resources for measurement in the same PRB(s) same symbol same subcell but different REs in TDD FR1 with eCPRI fronthaul when FD beamforming is activated:

* The two CSI-RS resources for measurement can be two CSI-RS row4 **or two CSI-RS row8.**
* The two CSI-RS for measurement have the same *antennaStream value, i.e. the two CSI-RS for measurement are in the same streams.*
* The two CSI-RS for measurement have the same *startPrb and* numOfPrb for DCM and **may have the same or different** *startPrb and* numOfPrb for WMP.***\****\*
* CSI-RS row4 frequency multiplexing with CSI-RS row8 in the same symbol is not supported but can be multiplexed in different symbols.

Note:

* when two CSI-RS resources for measurement are frequency multiplexed in the same PRB(s), the *numOfPrb of CSI-RS resource for measurement shall be reduced until the CSI-RS power does not exceed the maximum TX power, it is applied by CPRT. For details, refer to 5G CP Entity Architecture and Algorithms [11241136](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmsMe_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Frm%2Fcm%2Fstream%2F_EvoPVu3rEe-rL47x_rCCmw).*
* PDSCH rate matching around CSI-RS for measurement is not supported currently.

For supported *numOfPrb, refer to [11443408](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e_mDzfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).*

For supported CSI-RS for measurement, refer to [11443125](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e_k1rvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).

For supported *antennaStream, refer to [11444114](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e_puNPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) for CSI-RS row4 and [11444194](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e_qVNvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) for CSI-RS row8.*

As an example, the following figures show the multiplexing between two CSI-RS resources for measurement:

* Two CSI-RS row4 multiplexing in same PRB:
* *csiRsConfig = 4*
* *startSymbol = 13*
* *antennaStream = 0xF*
* *freqDomainAllocationKi of CSI-RS #1: 0000 0000 0001 (k0 = 0)*
* *freqDomainAllocationKi of CSI-RS #2: 0001 0000 0000 (k0 = 8)*

[image-0][image\_desc]The image displays a diagram illustrating the allocation of CSI-RS (Channel State Information Reference Signal) within an OFDM (Orthogonal Frequency-Division Multiplexing) symbol. The diagram is structured as a grid where the horizontal axis represents "OFDM symbol number" ranging from 0 to 13, and the vertical axis implicitly represents subcarriers within Physical Resource Blocks (PRBs).
Two CSI-RS resources are depicted: "CSI-RS #1" and "CSI-RS #2".
"CSI-RS #1" is shown as a blue and red triangular shape within the grid. The blue portion is at the bottom, and the red portion is above it. This resource spans across OFDM symbol numbers 0, 1, and 2. The label "CSI-RS #1" is positioned to the left of this resource. An arrow labeled "startPrb" points to the bottom edge of the grid, indicating the starting PRB. Another arrow labeled "startPrb + numOfPrb" points to the top edge of the grid, indicating the ending PRB. The text "One PRB" is also present, with a dashed box highlighting a small section within the CSI-RS #1 area, suggesting it represents a single PRB.
"CSI-RS #2" is depicted as a similar red and blue triangular shape, but it is positioned further to the right, spanning across OFDM symbol numbers 5, 6, and 7. The red portion is at the top, and the blue portion is below it. The label "CSI-RS #2" is placed to the right of this resource.
To the right of the main grid, there is a magnified view of a "subcarrier" column. This column is represented by a dashed rectangle containing several horizontal colored bars: red, blue, red, blue, red. This magnified view illustrates the subcarrier structure within a PRB, showing alternating red and blue subcarriers.
The diagram visually represents how CSI-RS resources are placed in terms of OFDM symbols and PRBs, and how they are composed of subcarriers.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_4986.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

For FR1 TDD, 5G-L1-DL shall support ssBurst signals frequency multiplexing with CSI-RS for beam management(s) in the same symbol(s) but different PRB(s) and same slot/subcell.

---

* The positions of CSI-RS subcarriers with respect to ssBurst subcarriers (above or below) are determined with the *startPrb and* numOfPrb parmeters provided by *DlData\_CsiRsSendReq ([11513061](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRuFePvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) message.*\*\*
* For each SSB burst blocks, 4 CSI-RS resources are used. The number of CSI-RS resources for beam management shall be multiple of 4.

As an example, the following figure shows the multiplexing between CSI-RS for beam management and ssBurst signals:

[image-0][image\_desc]The image displays a diagram illustrating the structure of a Synchronization Signal Block (SSB) in OFDM symbols, along with associated control channels and CSI-RS resources. The horizontal axis represents OFDM symbol numbers from 0 to 13. The vertical axis indicates resource allocation in terms of Physical Resource Blocks (PRBs), with labels like `ssBlockPrbOffset`, `startPrb + numOfPrb`, and `startPrb`.
The SSB itself occupies specific PRBs and OFDM symbols. Within the SSB, the following components are shown:
- A yellow block labeled "PSS" (Primary Synchronization Signal) is located in OFDM symbol 1.
- A green block labeled "PBCH/DMRS" (Physical Broadcast Channel / Demodulation Reference Signal) spans OFDM symbols 2 and 3.
- A blue block labeled "SSS" (Secondary Synchronization Signal) is in OFDM symbol 2.
- Another green block labeled "PBCH/DMRS" is in OFDM symbol 3.
Below the SSB, there are four red blocks labeled "#1", "#2", "#3", and "#4". These are indicated to be within the PRB range defined by `startPrb` and `startPrb + numOfPrb`.
A blue arrow originates from the area of these red blocks and points to a text box on the right. This text box states: "CSI-RS for beam management. 4 CSI-RS resources are transmitted for each SSB block". This suggests that these red blocks represent CSI-RS resources.
The diagram visually represents how different control and synchronization signals, as well as CSI-RS, are mapped onto the OFDM resource grid for a given SSB.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_4994.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

For FR2 TDD, 5G-L1-DL shall support to transmit the signal of CSI-RS for measurement in SSB slot with eCPRI fronthaul. The SCS of SSB is 240 kHz and the SCS of CSI-RS is 120 kHz.

## As an example, the following figure shows the multiplexing between CSI-RS for measurement with SSB case E:

[image-0][image\_desc]The image displays two diagrams illustrating the structure of 5G NR (New Radio) physical resource blocks (PRBs) within slots. Each diagram shows a breakdown of PRBs across multiple slots, highlighting the allocation of different channels.
The top diagram depicts two consecutive slots, labeled "N\_ss-slot #2j" and "N\_ss-slot #4j+1". Within these slots, there are sub-slots labeled "N\_us-slot #4j" and "N\_us-slot #4j+1". The PRBs are divided into smaller units called "SS/PBCH blocks". Specifically, "SS/PBCH block 0", "SS/PBCH block 1", "SS/PBCH block 2", and "SS/PBCH block 3" are shown. Each block contains a Primary Synchronization Signal (PSS), Secondary Synchronization Signal (SSS), and Physical Broadcast Channel with Demodulation Reference Signals (PBCH/DMRS). The diagram also indicates that 20 PRBs, each with 127 tones and a subcarrier spacing (SCS) of 240 kHz, are utilized. A CSI-RS (Channel State Information - Reference Signal) is shown to the right, with its starting position indicated by "startPrb" and its end by "startPrb + numOfPrb - 1". The SCS of CSI-RS is specified as 120 kHz.
The bottom diagram illustrates another pair of consecutive slots, labeled "N\_band-slot #2j+1" and "N\_band-slot #2j+1". These slots are further divided into sub-slots labeled "N\_us-slot #4j+2" and "N\_us-slot #4j+3". Similar to the top diagram, these sub-slots contain "SS/PBCH block 0", "SS/PBCH block 1", "SS/PBCH block 2", and "SS/PBCH block 3", each containing PSS, SSS, and PBCH/DMRS. The same PRB and SCS specifications (20 PRB of 127 tones, SCS = 240 kHz) are present. A CSI-RS is also shown on the right with the same start and end indicators and SCS.
The diagrams use color coding to differentiate between the PSS (yellow), SSS (light blue), and PBCH/DMRS (green) within the SS/PBCH blocks. The remaining parts of the PRBs are shown in a light orange/beige color. The numbering from 0 to 13 at the top of each sub-slot represents the resource element indices within that sub-slot.

| Thor BB | CPRI | Supported on {FDD} | - |
| 7-2a-eCPRI | Supported on {FDD, TDD-FR1, TDD-FR2} | Supported on {TDD-FR1} |  |
| Odin BB | CPRI | [**CB012115-JA, CB012115-JB]** Supported on {FDD} [End **CB012115-JA, CB012115-JB]** | - |
| 7-2a-eCPRI | [**CB012115-LA]** Supported on {FDD} [End **CB012115-LA]** [CB012115-IA] Supported on {TDD-FR1} [End CB012115-IA] | [CB012115-MD] (Parity from CB010602) Supported on {TDD-FR1} [End CB012115-MD] |  |

Note:

For CSI-RS power computation, see [11415882](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-ROHPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

#### 4.5.5.4.2 CSI-RS power setting

##### 4.5.5.4.2.1 CSI-RS power setting for CSI-RS for tracking

**4.5.5.4.2.1.0-3**  (ID: `12565781`)

CSI-RS power setting for CSI-RS for tracking
**CSI-RS power setting for CSI-RS for tracking:**

The parameter *pwrReductionPerCsiRsResource\_dB ([11513061](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRuFePvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) can be used to mute the CSI-RS for tracking.*

In non FD BF case (*actBeamforming is set to True, and either* dlEcpriFdBeamforming or *actDlEcpriPhase4  is set to False in* DlCell\_SetupReq message ([11512142](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRmwvfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G-L1-DL shall also support *pwrReductionPerCsiRsResource\_dB for CSI-RS for tracking*\*\*\*\*

The supported L1 HW(s) are shown in the following table:

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Technology | Loner | Loki | Thor BB | Odin BB |
| FR1-FDD-CPRI | Supported | Supported | Supported | **[CB012115-JA, CB012115-JB] Supported** [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-JB]\*\*\*\* |
| FR1-FDD-7-2a-eCPRI | Supported | Supported | Supported | **[CB012115-LA] Supported** [End CB012115-LA]\*\*\*\* |
| FR1-TDD-CPRI | Supported | Supported | Supported | - |
| FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI | Supported | Supported | Supported | **[CB012115-IA] Supported** [End CB012115-IA]\*\*\*\* |
| FR2-TDD-CPRI | Supported | - | - | - |
| FR2-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI | Supported | Supported | Supported | - |

---

##### 4.5.5.4.2.2 CSI-RS power setting for CSI-RS for measurement (acquisition)

**4.5.5.4.2.2.0-3**  (ID: `12565782`)

CSI-RS power setting for CSI-RS for measurement (acquisition)
**CSI-RS power setting for CSI-RS for acquisition (measurement):**

The power setting per RE for CSI-RS is the difference between two parameters *csiTransmitPower and* pwrReductionPerCsiRsResource\_dB received in *DlData\_CsiRsSendReq* *message from 5G-L2-PS.*\*\*\*\*

The parameter *pwrReductionPerCsiRsResource\_dB can be used to mute the CSI-RS for measurement.*

The supported L1 HW(s) are shown in the following table:

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Technology | Loner | Loki | Thor BB | Odin BB |
| FR1-FDD-CPRI | Supported | Supported | Supported | **[CB012115-SR-JA, CB012115-SR-JB] Supported** [End CB012115-SR-JA, CB012115-SR-JB]\*\*\*\* |
| FR1-FDD-7-2a-eCPRI | Supported | Supported | Supported | **[CB012115-SR-LA] Supported** [End CB012115-SR-LA]\*\*\*\* |
| FR1-TDD-CPRI | Supported | Supported | Supported | - |
| FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI | Supported | Supported | Supported | **[CB012115-SR-IA] Supported** [End CB012115-SR-IA]\*\*\*\* |
| FR2-TDD-CPRI | Supported | - | - | - |
| FR2-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI | Supported | Supported | Supported | - |

---

##### 4.5.5.4.2.3 CSI-RS power setting for ZP CSI-RS row5

**4.5.5.4.2.3.0-2**  (ID: `13420749`)

CSI-RS power setting for ZP CSI-RS row5
**CSI-RS power setting for ZP CSI-RS row5:**

For FR1 FDD DSS, **when the csiRsconfig=5 in *DlData\_CsiRsSendReq **message ([11513061](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRuFePvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), the parameter *pwrReductionPerCsiRsResource\_dB in* DlData\_CsiRsSendReq** message ([11513061](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRuFePvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is set to [51...255] to mute CSI-RS.*****\***\*

The supported L1 HW(s) are shown in the following table:

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Technology | Loner | Loki | Thor BB | Odin BB |
| FR1-FDD-CPRI | Supported | Supported | Supported | [CB012115-MA] (Parity from CB007738) Supported [End CB012115-MA] |
| FR1-FDD-7-2a-eCPRI | - | Supported | Supported | [CB012115-MA] (Parity from CB007738) Supported [End CB012115-MA] |

---

#### 4.5.5.4.3 CSI-RS power balance per beam

**4.5.5.4.3.0-5**  (ID: `13415294`)

CSI-RS power balance per beam
The supported CSI-RS configuration for CSI-RS power balance per beam are list in table below. For other configurations not list in the table, *csiBestBeamPowerOffset is set to 0.*

* IE csiRsPrecodingMatrix and IE csiBestBeamPowerOffset are provided by *DlData\_CsiRsSendReqL1sw (for SOC) message ([11513061](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRuFePvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for L1 BB.*

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| CSI-RS configuration | csiRsPrecodingMatrix | csiBestBeamPowerOffset |
| CSI-RS row4 | {0} | [0..150] |

The supported L1 HW(s) are shown in the following table:

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| L1 Hardware | Technology | CSI-RS row4 power balance per beam |
| Loner | FR1-TDD-CPRI, FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI | - |
| Loki | FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI | Supported |
| Thor BB | FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI | Supported |
| Odin BB | FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI | [CB012115-MD] (Parity from CB010602) Supported [End CB012115-MD] |

Note: For algorithm of CSI-RS power balance per beam, refer to [11416481](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-TqVfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) for Loki, [11416949](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-URYfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) for Thor.

---

### 4.5.5.5 CSI-RS real-timing beamforming weight computer

## 4.5.6 CSI-RS Capacity

### 4.5.6.1 Overview

**4.5.6.1.0-1**  (ID: `11444715`)

Overview
CSI-RS capacity stands for the maximum number of CSI-RS resources per slot per subcell. It refers to the IE *numOfCsiResources in* DlData\_CsiRsSendReq message ([11513061](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRuFePvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Note that this parameter does not exist explicitly, but instead can be obtained in MULTI implementation by csiRsResources.length\*\*

The total number of CSI-RS resources per subcell per slot shall lower or equal to the Maximum Number of CSI-RS resources per Subcell per slot.

**[CB007814-A] 5G-L1-DL shall also support *requirements above in ABIO for FR1 FDD eCPRI. \*\*[End CB007814-A]***\*\*

**[CB008205-B, CB008205-C] 5G-L1-DL shall also support requirements above in ABIO for O-RAN compliant FR1 FDD eCPRI.**[End CB008205-B, CB008205-C]\*\*\*\*

**[Before CNI-122313]**

**[CB009443] 5G-L1-DL shall also support SSB Case C for FR1 TDD eCPRI in RINLINE1.** [End CB009443]\*\*\*\*

**[CB009858-C] 5G-L1-DL shall also support SSB Case A for FR1 FDD eCPRI in RINLINE1.** [End CB009858-C]\*\*\*\*

**[CNI-122313] RINLINE 1 support is terminated in 24R1, requirement is not valid for RINLINE 1 starting from 24R2** [End CNI-122313]\*\*\*\*

---

**4.5.6.2.0-12**  (ID: `12461204`)

| 7-2a-eCPRI |  |  |  |

| 7-2a-eCPRI | 24 | 24 |  |
| Odin BB | CPRI | - | - |
| 7-2a-eCPRI | [CB012115-SR-IA] 1 [End CB012115-SR-IA] [CB012115-SR-MA] 24 [End CB012115-SR-MA] | [CB012115-SR-IB] 1 [End CB012115-SR-IB] [CB012115-SR-MA] 24 [End CB012115-SR-MA] |  |
